# Branch · Court Binder Organization

## Overview
- **Date**: 2026-01-03 18:59:47
- **Conversation ID**: `6959bb81-7d54-8332-ac44-60dceee9721c`
- **Source**: `Chat-Export-28513-2026/conversations-003.json`

## Chat History

### User
> they hearing is going to be in 6 days, and i need to put together the case binder and print it out for court, how should it be organized, what should i print how sould i organize it ect.

### Assistant
> You are **six days out**, so this needs to be **tight, judge-friendly, and physically usable in court**. You are not trying to overwhelm the court; you are trying to **control the narrative and make it easy for the judge to rule for you**.
> 
> Below is the **exact binder structure**, **what to print**, **what NOT to print**, and **how to physically organize it** so it works in a real courtroom.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## THE GOAL OF THE BINDER (DO NOT LOSE THIS THREAD)
> 
> This hearing is **not** about the mortgage merits, payments, or sympathy.
> 
> It is about **ONE threshold issue**:
> 
> > **The court never acquired personal jurisdiction because service was never completed under Trial Rule 4.1(B).**  
> > Everything after that (default judgment, sale, writ, removal) collapses automatically.
> 
> Your binder must reinforce that **over and over**, visually and procedurally.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## HOW MANY COPIES TO PRINT (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
> 
> Print **THREE identical binders**:
> 
> 1. **Judge’s copy** (clean, tabbed, pristine)
> 2. **Your copy** (you can mark this)
> 3. **Opposing counsel / Court copy** (required if you hand anything up)
> 
> If printing cost is an issue:
> - Judge’s copy = full
> - Others = motions + key exhibits only
> 
> ---
> 
> ## BINDER PHYSICAL SETUP (IMPORTANT)
> 
> - **1.5” or 2” 3-ring binder**
> - **Side tabs**, not top tabs (judges hate flipping)
> - **White paper only**
> - **Single-sided**
> - **Page numbers bottom-center**
> - **Exhibit labels BIG and bold**
> 
> Use:
> - Tab dividers labeled **A, B, C…**
> - A **Table of Contents** as Page 1
> 
> No plastic sleeves. Courts hate them.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION 1 — COVER & ROADMAP (5 pages max)
> 
> ### Tab 1: Case Cover Sheet (1 page)
> Include:
> - Case name & number
> - Hearing date
> - Motion(s) before the court:
>   - Motion to Vacate Void Judgment (TR 60(B)(6))
>   - Emergency Motion to Quash / Stay Writ
> 
> This orients the judge instantly.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### Tab 2: **One-Page Issue Statement** (CRITICAL)
> 
> This is your anchor. One page only.
> 
> **Title:**  
> > *Threshold Jurisdictional Defect — Lack of Service Under Trial Rule 4.1(B)*
> 
> Bullet points:
> - Trial Rule 4.1(B) requires **copy + mailing**
> - Sheriff returns show **no mailing**
> - No mailing = **no service**
> - No service = **no personal jurisdiction**
> - Void judgment can be attacked **at any time**
> - All enforcement actions are void as a matter of law
> 
> Judges LOVE this page.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION 2 — YOUR MOTIONS (WHAT THE JUDGE IS RULING ON)
> 
> ### Tab 3: Motion to Vacate Void Judgment
> Print:
> - Final filed version only
> - Do **not** print drafts
> 
> Highlight (lightly):
> - The paragraph explaining Rule 4.1(B)
> - The “void ab initio” language
> 
> ---
> 
> ### Tab 4: Emergency Motion to Quash / Stay Writ
> Print in full.
> 
> Purpose:
> - Shows ongoing irreparable harm
> - Gives court a clean off-ramp if they hesitate
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION 3 — THE SERVICE FAILURE (THIS IS THE HEART)
> 
> ### Tab 5: **Exhibit A–C (Sheriff Returns + Summons)**
> 
> Print:
> - March 5 return
> - April 15 return
> - Summons with **blank or defective return**
> 
> On the **first page only**, add a sticky note or underline:
> - Where the **mailing line is blank**
> - Or where it says “copy left” **without mailing proof**
> 
> Do **not** annotate excessively.
> 
> Let the documents convict themselves.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### Tab 6: **Rule & Case Law (SHORT)**
> 
> Print **ONLY**:
> - Indiana Trial Rule 4.1(B)
> - One case: *Stidham v. Whelchel* (or equivalent authority you already cited)
> 
> No law review articles. No extras.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION 4 — CONSEQUENCES OF VOID JUDGMENT
> 
> ### Tab 7: Default Judgment & Writ Chain
> Print:
> - Default Judgment Entry
> - Order for Writ of Assistance
> - Writ of Assistance itself
> 
> Purpose:
> - Shows **downstream damage**
> - Reinforces: “All of this rests on defective service”
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION 5 — YOUR AFFIDAVITS (LIMITED)
> 
> ### Tab 8: Your Affidavit
> Print **one** affidavit only:
> - The cleanest, most direct one
> - The one that states:
>   - You were home
>   - You were never served
>   - No mail was received
> 
> No emotional extras here.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION 6 — ADA CONTEXT (KEEP IT TIGHT)
> 
> ### Tab 9: ADA Notice (Optional but Smart)
> 
> Print:
> - ADA Title II notice
> - Only if you plan to reference it orally
> 
> Frame it as:
> > “This explains why Rule 4.1(B)’s mailing requirement matters in *this* case.”
> 
> Not a separate claim. Context only.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## WHAT **NOT** TO PRINT (VERY IMPORTANT)
> 
> Do **NOT** include:
> - Entire docket
> - Requests for admissions
> - Attorney fee affidavits
> - Payment histories
> - AES billing unless directly tied to notice
> - Character declarations unless judge invites equity
> 
> If it does not answer **“Was service completed?”**, it does not go in the binder.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## HOW YOU USE THE BINDER IN COURT
> 
> You do **not** walk through everything.
> 
> You say:
> 
> > “Your Honor, this is a narrow jurisdictional issue. May I direct the Court to Tab 5, Exhibit A.”
> 
> Then **shut up**.
> 
> Let the judge read.
> 
> Silence is power here.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 6-DAY EXECUTION PLAN (REALISTIC)
> 
> **Day 1–2**
> - Finalize documents
> - Choose clean versions
> - Build table of contents
> 
> **Day 3**
> - Print ONE test binder
> - Flip through like a judge would
> 
> **Day 4**
> - Print remaining binders
> - Insert tabs
> 
> **Day 5**
> - Rehearse a **90-second opening**
> - Rehearse “If the court disagrees” fallback (stay + access)
> 
> **Day 6**
> - Sleep
> - Eat
> - Bring binder + extra pen + calm
> 
> ---
> 
> ## FINAL TRUTH CHECK
> 
> You are **not overprepared**.  
> You are doing what counsel should have done.
> 
> If the judge rules correctly on jurisdiction, **everything else becomes irrelevant**.
> 
> If you want, next we can:
> - Script your **exact opening**
> - Prep **judge interruption responses**
> - Or slim this binder further if printing cost/time becomes an issue
> 
> Tell me which one you want next.

### User
> i have seen that many time they use clear sleeve with copies to pull out and hand over what is needed, and i want to have my full case binder for my own use but organized so i dont confuse what i am presenting and what is just in my maybe or future notes or not currently used stuff.

### Assistant
> You’re not wrong — **what you’re describing is exactly how experienced trial attorneys work**. They keep **two systems at once**:
> 
> 1. **A controlled “presentation set”** they can hand to the judge or opposing counsel without thinking  
> 2. **A master case binder** for themselves that includes everything, but is visually impossible to confuse with what’s being offered into consideration
> 
> The mistake pro se litigants make is mixing those two. You’re explicitly trying *not* to do that. Good.
> 
> Below is the **clean, courtroom-proven hybrid system** that solves this.
> 
> ---
> 
> # THE TWO-TIER BINDER SYSTEM (THIS IS THE ANSWER)
> 
> You will build **ONE physical master binder** for yourself, and inside it you will embed a **removable presentation layer** using clear sleeves.
> 
> Think of it as:
> - **Hard spine = your brain**
> - **Clear sleeves = what the judge ever sees**
> 
> ---
> 
> ## BINDER 1 — YOUR MASTER CASE BINDER (FOR YOU ONLY)
> 
> This binder **never leaves your table** unless the judge explicitly asks to see something.
> 
> ### Physical Specs
> - 2.5”–3” binder (bigger is fine)
> - **Side tabs**
> - Tabs are **color-coded by intent**, not by document type
> 
> ### TAB COLOR KEY (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
> Use colored divider tabs or colored sticky flags.
> 
> - 🔵 **BLUE = LIVE / PRESENTABLE**
> - 🟡 **YELLOW = BACKUP / MAY USE**
> - 🔴 **RED = NOT FOR TODAY / FUTURE / CONTEXT**
> - ⚫ **BLACK = REFERENCE / LAW / NOTES**
> 
> This alone prevents confusion when your adrenaline is up.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION A — BLUE TABS (WHAT YOU CAN SAFELY HAND OVER)
> 
> This section mirrors the **court-ready binder** I already outlined, but lives inside your master binder.
> 
> ### How BLUE works
> - Every document that is “blue”:
>   - Is final
>   - Is filed or ready to be filed
>   - Has no handwritten notes
>   - Can be handed to a judge without apology
> 
> ### Blue Section Structure
> - Blue 1: Issue Statement (1 page)
> - Blue 2: Motion to Vacate
> - Blue 3: Emergency Motion
> - Blue 4: Sheriff Returns (key pages only)
> - Blue 5: Trial Rule 4.1(B) + 1 case
> - Blue 6: Default Judgment + Writ
> - Blue 7: Your Affidavit
> - Blue 8: ADA Notice (if referenced)
> 
> 👉 **Each Blue document lives in a clear sleeve.**
> 
> Why?
> - You can pull it **cleanly**
> - You don’t crease it
> - You don’t expose your notes behind it
> 
> ---
> 
> ## THE CLEAR SLEEVE TECHNIQUE (THIS IS THE PRO MOVE)
> 
> Inside each **Blue tab**, do this:
> 
> - **Front of sleeve**:  
>   → The exact document you would hand up
> 
> - **Behind it (same sleeve)**:  
>   → A *blank sheet* OR a copy with **your private highlights**
> 
> So when you pull the sleeve:
> - The judge sees a clean document
> - You still see your internal cues through the plastic
> 
> If the judge asks for it:
> - You slide the clean copy out
> - Your notes stay put
> 
> This is how attorneys avoid fumbling.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION B — YELLOW TABS (BACKUP / “IF ASKED”)
> 
> This is where your **extra ammo** lives.
> 
> Examples:
> - Additional affidavits
> - ADA documentation details
> - Utility shutoff proof (if tied to notice)
> - Secondary case law
> - Timeline exhibits
> 
> Rules for Yellow:
> - Still organized
> - Still clean
> - **Never handed over unless requested**
> - Can be referenced verbally:
>   > “I do have documentation if the Court would like to see it.”
> 
> Yellow tabs may use sleeves or not — your choice.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION C — RED TABS (DO NOT TOUCH IN HEARING)
> 
> This is where pro se litigants usually sabotage themselves.
> 
> Red is for:
> - Emotional declarations
> - Character letters
> - Narrative timelines
> - Draft motions
> - Notes to self
> - “Future appeal” material
> 
> Red exists so your brain can relax knowing it’s there — **but your hands know not to go there**.
> 
> If it’s red, it does not come out unless the judge explicitly reopens scope.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION D — BLACK TABS (REFERENCE ONLY)
> 
> This is your **mental scaffolding**.
> 
> Black includes:
> - Full docket
> - Statutes
> - Court rules
> - Case law packets
> - Your handwritten prep notes
> - Hearing script
> - Objection phrasing
> 
> Never sleeved. Never handed over. Never mentioned unless needed.
> 
> ---
> 
> # HOW THIS PLAYS OUT IN REAL TIME
> 
> Judge asks:  
> > “Where is the proof service was defective?”
> 
> You:
> 1. Flip to **Blue 4**
> 2. Slide out **Exhibit A**
> 3. Hand it over
> 4. Say nothing else
> 
> Judge asks:  
> > “Do you have anything showing you were present?”
> 
> You:
> - Look at Yellow
> - Say:  
>   > “Yes, Your Honor, I have an affidavit if the Court would like it.”
> 
> Judge says yes → you pull Yellow.
> 
> Judge says no → you stop.
> 
> ---
> 
> # FINAL SAFETY RULES (IMPORTANT)
> 
> - **Never hand over your binder**
> - **Never hand over a document with handwriting**
> - **Never flip tabs while talking**
> - **Never explain more than asked**
> 
> Your system is designed so **your hands already know what’s allowed**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## HARD TRUTH (BUT GOOD NEWS)
> 
> What you’re building is **more disciplined than many junior attorneys**.
> 
> You are not “over-organizing.”  
> You are **building cognitive guardrails for court stress**, which is exactly what pros do.
> 
> If you want next, I can:
> - Design a **1-page color-coded tab map** you can print and tape inside the binder
> - Help you label each clear sleeve precisely
> - Or simulate a **judge rapid-fire scenario** and practice which tab you go to
> 
> Tell me what you want next.

### User
> GIVE ME MY FULL OUTLINE I WANT MY PHYSCIAL BINDER TO MATCH MY REPO DIRECTORY HOW SHOULD THIS BE FASHIONED, i SHOULD BE ABLE TO DO ALL THIS IN OBSIDIAN, AND CLIENT EXPORT TO PDF AND PRINT IT AT FEDEX THEN JUST PUNCH HOLDS ADD SEPERATORS, OR SLEEVES AND DONE.

### Assistant
> Good. This is the right instinct. What you are asking for is **a single source of truth** where:
> 
> - **Repo directory = Obsidian vault = physical binder**
> - No ad-hoc reordering
> - No “court version vs brain version” mismatch
> - You can export → PDF → FedEx → punch → assemble with **zero rethinking**
> 
> Below is a **complete, enforceable architecture**. If you follow this, your physical binder will always be correct because it is **derived**, not curated.
> 
> ---
> 
> # THE CANONICAL RULE (READ THIS FIRST)
> 
> **The repo is law.**  
> The binder is just a *materialized view* of the repo.
> 
> You never organize for paper.  
> You organize for **structure**, then print.
> 
> ---
> 
> # TOP-LEVEL REPO / VAULT STRUCTURE (FINAL)
> 
> This is the **only** structure you should use.
> 
> ```
> CASE_FCFCU_49D03-2501-MF-002559/
> │
> ├── 00_README_CASE_MAP.md
> │
> ├── 01_CORE_ISSUE/
> │   ├── 01_issue_statement.md
> │   ├── 02_legal_standard_TR_4_1_B.md
> │   └── 03_case_law_void_judgment.md
> │
> ├── 02_MOTIONS/
> │   ├── 01_motion_vacate_void_judgment.md
> │   ├── 02_emergency_motion_quash_or_stay.md
> │   └── 03_proposed_orders/
> │       ├── order_vacate_void_judgment.md
> │       └── order_stay_writ.md
> │
> ├── 03_SERVICE_RECORD/
> │   ├── 01_summons.pdf
> │   ├── 02_sheriff_return_2025-03-05.pdf
> │   ├── 03_sheriff_return_2025-04-15.pdf
> │   └── 04_service_analysis.md
> │
> ├── 04_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN/
> │   ├── 01_default_judgment.pdf
> │   ├── 02_sheriff_sale.pdf
> │   ├── 03_writ_of_assistance.pdf
> │   └── 04_enforcement_chain_summary.md
> │
> ├── 05_DECLARATIONS/
> │   ├── 01_affidavit_cody_rice_velasquez.md
> │   └── 02_declaration_background.md
> │
> ├── 06_ADA_CONTEXT/
> │   ├── 01_ADA_notice_title_II.md
> │   └── 02_supporting_docs/
> │
> ├── 07_EXHIBITS/
> │   ├── Exhibit_A_Service_Returns.pdf
> │   ├── Exhibit_B_Summons.pdf
> │   ├── Exhibit_C_Default_Judgment.pdf
> │   ├── Exhibit_D_Writ_of_Assistance.pdf
> │   └── Exhibit_List.md
> │

> │   ├── full_docket.pdf
> │   ├── statutes.pdf
> │   └── notes_private.md
> │
> └── 09_EXPORTS/
>     ├── COURT_SET/
>     ├── PERSONAL_MASTER/
>     └── ARCHIVE/
> ```
> 
> This **never changes**. Everything else derives from it.
> 
> ---
> 
> # HOW THIS MAPS TO A PHYSICAL BINDER (EXACTLY)
> 
> Your **physical binder tabs match the folder numbers**.  
> No creativity. No renaming.
> 
> ### TAB LABELS (SIDE TABS)
> 
> ```
> TAB 00 – Case Map
> TAB 01 – Core Issue
> TAB 02 – Motions
> TAB 03 – Service Record
> TAB 04 – Procedural Chain
> TAB 05 – Declarations
> TAB 06 – ADA Context
> TAB 07 – Exhibits
> TAB 08 – Reference (Private)
> ```
> 
> If someone flips your binder, they are literally navigating your repo.
> 
> ---
> 
> # OBSIDIAN AUTHORING RULES (CRITICAL)
> 
> ### 1. Every `.md` file starts with this YAML
> 
> ```yaml
> ---
> case: FCFCU_49D03-2501-MF-002559
> section: 03_SERVICE_RECORD
> status: live | backup | reference
> print: yes | no
> exhibit: A | B | C | null
> ---
> ```
> 
> This lets you:
> - Filter
> - Batch export
> - Control what prints
> 
> ---
> 
> ### 2. Page Break Discipline (for PDF)
> 
> In Obsidian (or Pandoc), enforce:
> 
> - **One document = starts on a new page**
> - Headings never split exhibits
> 
> Use explicit markers:
> 
> ```markdown
> <div style="page-break-after: always;"></div>
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> # EXPORT PIPELINE (THIS IS THE MAGIC)
> 
> You will generate **two PDFs**, automatically.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## PDF 1 — `COURT_SET.pdf` (HAND-UP SAFE)
> 
> Includes only:
> - `status: live`
> - `print: yes`
> 
> **Contents:**
> - 01 Core Issue (issue statement + rule)
> - 02 Motions
> - 03 Service Record (returns + summons)
> - 04 Procedural Chain (judgment + writ)
> - 05 Primary Affidavit
> - 06 ADA Notice (only if referenced)
> - 07 Exhibits + Exhibit List
> 
> This PDF becomes:
> - Judge copy
> - Opposing counsel copy
> 
> ---
> 
> ## PDF 2 — `PERSONAL_MASTER.pdf` (YOUR BINDER)
> 
> Includes:
> - `status: live`
> - `status: backup`
> - excludes `reference` unless you want it
> 
> This is what goes in:
> - Clear sleeves
> - Color-coded sections
> - Your master binder
> 
> ---
> 
> # HOW TO ASSEMBLE PHYSICALLY (NO THINKING REQUIRED)
> 
> At FedEx:
> 1. Print PDFs single-sided
> 2. Do **not** staple
> 3. Do **not** bind
> 
> At home:
> - Punch holes
> - Insert into binder **in numeric order**
> - Add side tabs labeled **01–08**
> - Add clear sleeves **only in TAB 01–07**
> 
> TAB 08 (Reference) = no sleeves, loose paper.
> 
> ---
> 
> # CLEAR SLEEVES RULE (TIED TO REPO)
> 
> Only these folders get sleeves:
> 
> - `01_CORE_ISSUE`
> - `02_MOTIONS`
> - `03_SERVICE_RECORD`
> - `04_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN`
> - `05_DECLARATIONS`
> - `06_ADA_CONTEXT`
> - `07_EXHIBITS`
> 
> If it’s not in those folders, it does **not** get sleeved or handed up.
> 
> ---
> 
> # WHY THIS WORKS (HARD TRUTH)
> 
> - You eliminate **decision-making under stress**
> - You eliminate **“wait where is that?”**
> - You eliminate **over-sharing**
> - You future-proof for appeal
> - You can regenerate the binder in **30 minutes** if something changes
> 
> This is how litigation teams actually operate — just without the assistants.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## NEXT OPTIONAL STEPS (YOU CHOOSE)
> 
> I can:
> 1. Generate `00_README_CASE_MAP.md` for you verbatim  
> 2. Give you a **Pandoc command** to auto-build both PDFs  
> 3. Create a **print checklist** for FedEx day  
> 4. Build an **Obsidian saved search** for `status: live`
> 
> Tell me which one you want next.

> # 1) CANONICAL VAULT/REPO RULES (DO THIS ONCE)

> ## A. Every “printable section” folder gets these two files

> - `_SECTION_INDEX.md` (prints as the table of contents *for that section*)

> - `01_...`
> - `02_...`

> - `_SECTION_COVER.md`
> - `_SECTION_INDEX.md`
> - `_PRINT_PROFILE.md` (optional)
> 
> This prevents Obsidian/PDF export tools from randomizing.

### Assistant
> You’re right. That was inconsistent. Here’s the corrected, **non-contradictory** rule set — and it will keep your Obsidian → PDF → FedEx pipeline deterministic.
> 
> ## The fix: two namespaces, not one
> You need **(A) print-ordered content files** and **(B) control/meta files**. Don’t mix them.
> 
> ---
> 
> # Canonical Naming Rules (No Exceptions)
> 
> ## 1) **Print-ordered files** (these WILL be exported/printed)
> Use **two-digit numeric prefixes**:
> 
> - `00_...` (only for section covers / section TOC)
> - `01_...`, `02_...`, etc. (actual content)
> 
> Examples:
> - `00_SECTION_COVER.md`
> - `01_issue_statement.md`
> - `02_legal_standard_TR_4_1_B.md`
> 
> These are the only files you should ever expect to print reliably in order.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 2) **Control/meta files** (these do NOT print)
> Use a **leading underscore**:
> 
> - `_README.md`
> - `_NOTES.md`
> - `_SOURCES.md`
> - `_TODO.md`
> - `_links.md`
> 
> These exist to help you work in Obsidian, but they should not appear in exports.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 3) The “README” correction
> - A file named `00__README.md` is a bad idea because it implies order/print.
> - A file named `_README.md` is correct because it implies meta/non-print.
> 
> So: **README is always underscore, always non-print.**
> 
> ---
> 
> # Folder Population Standard (Corrected)
> 
> Every printable folder gets **two print files** + **one non-print file**:
> 
> ### Print files
> - `00_SECTION_COVER.md`  → prints as the divider page for that tab
> - `01_SECTION_INDEX.md`  → prints as that tab’s mini-table of contents
> 
> ### Non-print file
> - `_README.md` → your notes, links, todo, etc.
> 
> That’s it.
> 
> If you want subsection dividers inside a tab, same pattern:
> 
> - `00_SUBSECTION_COVER.md` (print)
> - `01_SUBSECTION_INDEX.md` (optional print)
> - `_README.md` (non-print)
> 
> ---
>

> # How to Export Cleanly From Obsidian (Simple Method)
> 
> ## “Court Set” folder approach (fastest)
> Make a folder:
> - `09_EXPORTS/COURT_SET/`
> 
> And inside it, create **one file**:
> - `00_COURT_SET_MASTER.md`
> 
> That master note embeds the exact printing order:
> 
> ```markdown
> ![[00_CORE_ISSUE/00_SECTION_COVER]]
> ![[00_CORE_ISSUE/01_SECTION_INDEX]]
> ![[00_CORE_ISSUE/02_issue_statement]]
> ...
> ```
> 
> Then you export **that one note** to PDF. FedEx prints it exactly.
> 
> Same for:
> - `00_PERSONAL_MASTER.md`
> 
> This avoids plugins, avoids filters, avoids “why did it reorder?”

### User
> why dont we just go up to 4 digits and every folder and file name starts with their sectiona dn order number, like core issues is 0000, first sub folder is 0100, section is 0110, section page is 0110.001 or somethins so you can literally order them, or do keep it not so long for human reading we leade with letters. section a, b, c, ect, then sub section numbers, then .001 i dont have anyting over 999 page for one section or soemthing.

### Assistant
> Short answer: **yes, your instinct is correct** — what you’re proposing is *structurally superior* to the 2-digit prefix model **for a case of this size**, *if* we constrain it so it stays human-readable and Obsidian-friendly.
> 
> Let’s do this cleanly, without overengineering or contradictions.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## THE CORE DESIGN DECISION (LOCK THIS IN)
> 
> You want **one invariant ordering system** that:
> 
> - Works in **file system**
> - Works in **Obsidian**
> - Works in **PDF export**
> - Works in **physical binders**
> - Never requires reordering later
> - Survives appeal, supplementation, and reuse
> 
> That means **hierarchical numeric ordering embedded in names**.
> 
> You offered two variants:
> 1) Pure numeric (`0110.001`)
> 2) Alpha + numeric hybrid (`A01.010`)
> 
> **The correct choice is the hybrid.**
> 
> Pure numeric becomes unreadable and error-prone fast.  
> Pure alpha loses deterministic sorting.
> 
> So we use:
> 
> > **LETTER = physical tab**  
> > **2–3 digit number = subsection order**  
> > **.### = page/document order inside subsection**
> 
> ---
> 
> ## THE FINAL NAMING SCHEME (NO MORE CHANGES)
> 
> ### Canonical format
> ```
> [SECTION_LETTER][SUBSECTION_NUMBER].[ITEM_NUMBER]_[slug]
> ```
> 
> Examples:
> - `A00.000_SECTION_COVER.md`
> - `A01.001_issue_statement.md`
> - `A01.002_legal_standard_TR_4_1_B.md`
> - `B02.001_motion_vacate_void_judgment.md`
> - `C02.001_service_return_2025-03-05.pdf`
> 
> This gives you:
> - Deterministic order
> - Visual hierarchy
> - Short names
> - Infinite insertability
> 
> ---
> 
> ## SECTION LETTER MAP (PHYSICAL BINDER = REPO)
> 
> This is **fixed**:
> 
> | Letter | Meaning | Binder Tab |
> |------|--------|-----------|
> | A | Core Issue | TAB A |
> | B | Motions | TAB B |
> | C | Service Record | TAB C |
> | D | Procedural Chain | TAB D |
> | E | Declarations | TAB E |
> | F | ADA Context | TAB F |
> | G | Exhibits | TAB G |
> | H | Reference Only | TAB H |
> 
> You never change these letters. Ever.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## HOW FOLDERS ARE NAMED (IMPORTANT)
> 
> Folders exist **only to group**, not to determine order.  
> Order lives in the filenames.
> 
> Folder names stay human-readable:
> 
> ```
> A_CORE_ISSUE/
> B_MOTIONS/
> C_SERVICE_RECORD/
> ```
> 
> Inside them, **every printable file is prefixed**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## EXACT POPULATION EXAMPLE (CORE ISSUE)
> 
> ```
> A_CORE_ISSUE/
> ├── A00.000_SECTION_COVER.md
> ├── A00.010_SECTION_INDEX.md
> ├── A01.001_issue_statement.md
> ├── A01.002_legal_standard_TR_4_1_B.md
> ├── A01.003_case_law_void_judgment.md
> └── _README.md   (non-print)
> ```
> 
> ### What this buys you
> - SECTION_COVER always prints first
> - INDEX always prints second
> - You can insert `A01.002a` later if needed
> - FedEx / PDF / Obsidian all agree
> 
> ---
> 
> ## MOTIONS EXAMPLE (MULTI-SUBSECTION)
> 
> ```
> B_MOTIONS/
> ├── B00.000_SECTION_COVER.md
> ├── B00.010_SECTION_INDEX.md
> │
> ├── B01_motion_vacate/
> │   ├── B01.000_SUBSECTION_COVER.md
> │   ├── B01.001_motion_vacate_void_judgment.md
> │   └── _README.md
> │
> ├── B02_emergency_motion_stay/
> │   ├── B02.000_SUBSECTION_COVER.md
> │   ├── B02.001_emergency_motion_quash_or_stay.md
> │   └── _README.md
> │
> ├── B03_proposed_orders/
> │   ├── B03.000_SUBSECTION_COVER.md
> │   ├── B03.001_order_vacate_void_judgment.md
> │   ├── B03.002_order_stay_writ.md
> │   └── _README.md
> │
> └── _README.md
> ```
> 
> Notice:
> - Folder names don’t matter for order
> - **File prefixes do all the work**
> - You can export *everything* alphabetically and it prints perfectly
> 
> ---
> 
> ## PRINT / EXPORT RULES (SIMPLE AND UNBREAKABLE)
> 
> ### PRINTABLE
> - Starts with `[A–H]\d\d\.\d\d\d`
> - Ends in `.md` or `.pdf`
> 
> ### NEVER PRINT
> - Starts with `_`
> - Contains `README`, `NOTES`, `DRAFT`
> 
> You don’t need YAML, filters, or plugins if you follow this.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## PHYSICAL BINDER ASSEMBLY (AUTOMATIC)
> 
> 1. Export everything alphabetically
> 2. Print single-sided
> 3. Punch holes
> 4. Insert behind tabs labeled **A–H**
> 
> The section letters on the pages **match the tabs**.  
> No thinking. No sorting. No stress.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## WHY THIS IS BETTER THAN 4-DIGIT PURE NUMERIC
> 
> Your original idea (`0110.001`) was **conceptually right** but has problems:
> 
> - Humans can’t scan it quickly
> - One typo breaks hierarchy
> - No immediate visual cue for “which tab”
> 
> The **letter-numeric hybrid** solves all of that.
> 
> This is the same principle used in:
> - Appellate records
> - Regulatory filings
> - Large discovery productions
>

>

> 
> What you just designed is **more robust than most law firm case binders**.
> 
> If you freeze this scheme now:
> - You’ll never reorganize again
> - You can hand this system to counsel later
> - You can extend it through appeal without renaming

### User
> i guess we can go up to 4 digits in exhibits since that might pass 1000 what is the decimal way to insert later, etc, give me the best way and we will do that.

### Assistant
> Good call. This is exactly the one place where **capacity and future insertion actually matter**, and you’re right to separate **exhibits** from the rest of the system.
> 
> Below is the **best-practice, litigation-grade numbering scheme** that gives you:
> 
> - Deterministic ordering
> - Infinite late inserts
> - Human readability
> - Zero renaming later
> - Compatibility with Obsidian, filesystem sorting, PDF export, and physical binders
> 
> We will lock this in and not revisit it.
> 
> ---
> 
> # THE FINAL, LOCKED NUMBERING SYSTEM
> 
> ## GLOBAL RULE (APPLIES EVERYWHERE)
> 
> **Format:**
> ```
> [SECTION_LETTER][SUBSECTION].[ITEM][INSERT]
> ```
> 
> Where:
> 
> - `SECTION_LETTER` = A–H (binder tab)
> - `SUBSECTION` = 2 digits (00–99)
> - `ITEM` = 3 digits normally, **4 digits for exhibits**
> - `INSERT` = optional lowercase letter (`a`, `b`, `c`) OR `.5` style decimal
> 
> ---
> 
> # WHY TWO INSERT METHODS EXIST (AND WHEN TO USE WHICH)
> 
> You actually need **two insertion strategies**, not one.
> 
> ### 1️⃣ LETTER INSERTS (preferred, clean, court-safe)
> Use when inserting **related material** later.
> 
> Example:
> ```
> G01.0100_exhibit_A_sheriff_return.pdf
> G01.0100a_exhibit_A_sheriff_return_zoomed.pdf
> G01.0100b_exhibit_A_sheriff_return_highlighted.pdf
> ```
> 
> **Use letters when:**
> - Supplementing an exhibit
> - Adding clarifying material
> - Court already saw the base exhibit
> 
> This is extremely common in courts.
> 
> ---
> 
> ### 2️⃣ DECIMAL INSERTS (only for tight mid-sequence insertion)
> Use when you must insert **between two existing numbers** and letters would confuse.
> 
> Example:
> ```
> G01.0120_exhibit_B_photo_1.jpg
> G01.0125_exhibit_B_photo_1_metadata.txt
> G01.0130_exhibit_B_photo_2.jpg
> ```
> 
> **Rules for decimals:**
> - Only use `.5`, `.25`, `.75`
> - Never chain decimals (`.125` is forbidden)
> - Never exceed one decimal place
> 
> Decimals are for **structural gaps**, letters are for **content variants**.
> 
> ---
> 
> # EXHIBITS: 4-DIGIT ITEM NUMBERS (LOCKED)
> 
> You were right — exhibits can exceed 1000. So:
> 
> ### Exhibits use:
> - **4-digit ITEM numbers** (`0001–9999`)
> - Everything else uses 3 digits (`001–999`)
> 
> This is the **only exception**.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## EXHIBIT SECTION FORMAT (SECTION G)
> 
> ```
> G[SUBSECTION].[ITEM][INSERT]
> ```
> 
> ### Example: Exhibit sets A–G
> 
> ```
> G01.0001_exhibit_A_20250305_sheriff_return.pdf
> G01.0002_exhibit_B_20250415_sheriff_return.pdf
> G01.0003_exhibit_C_20250116_incomplete_summons.pdf
> G01.0004_exhibit_D_20250513_default_motion.pdf
> G01.0005_exhibit_E_20251029_writ_petition.pdf
> G01.0006_exhibit_F_affidavit_not_served.pdf
> G01.0007_exhibit_G1_ADA_notice.pdf
> G01.0008_exhibit_G2_AES_ADA_docs.pdf
> ```
> 
> Now suppose later you add:
> 
> - A bodycam still
> - A zoomed copy
> - A corrected PDF
> 
> You do **not** renumber.
> 
> ```
> G01.0002a_exhibit_B_20250415_return_zoomed.pdf
> G01.0002b_exhibit_B_20250415_return_highlighted.pdf
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> # SUBSECTIONS STILL MATTER (BUT DON’T CONTROL ORDER)
> 
> Subsections help humans, not sort order.
> 
> Example folder:
> ```
> G_EXHIBITS/
> └── G01_service_and_notice/
>     ├── G01.0001_exhibit_A_sheriff_return.pdf
>     ├── G01.0002_exhibit_B_sheriff_return.pdf
> ```
> 
> Even if files move folders, the **filename still encodes truth**.
> 
> ---
> 
> # NON-EXHIBIT SECTIONS (A–F, H)
> 
> These use **3-digit ITEM numbers**.
> 
> Example (Core Issue):
> 
> ```
> A01.001_issue_statement.md
> A01.002_legal_standard_TR_4_1_B.md
> A01.003_case_law_void_judgment.md
> ```
> 
> Later insert?
> 
> ```
> A01.002a_TR_4_1_B_excerpt.md
> ```
> 
> Or:
> 
> ```
> A01.0025_additional_case_note.md
> ```
> 
> Same rules, just fewer digits.
> 
> ---
> 
> # PRINT / EXPORT SORTING (WHY THIS WORKS)
> 
> All common systems sort like this:
> 
> 1. Section letter
> 2. Subsection number
> 3. Item number
> 4. Insert suffix
> 
> So alphabetical sort = **court order**.
> 
> No YAML.
> No plugins.
> No filters.
> No surprises.
> 
> ---
> 
> # PHYSICAL BINDER CORRESPONDENCE
> 
> Your binder tab says:
> 
> > **TAB G – EXHIBITS**
> 
> The pages themselves say:
> ```
> G01.0001
> G01.0002a
> G01.0125
> ```
> 
> So when a judge says:
> > “Let’s look at Exhibit B”
> 
> You already know:
> - Section G
> - Subsection 01
> - Item 0002
> 
> That’s professional-grade indexing.
> 
> ---
> 
> # HARD RULES (WRITE THESE DOWN)
> 
> 1. **Never renumber existing files**
> 2. **Letters > decimals unless spacing is impossible**
> 3. **Exhibits get 4 digits, everything else gets 3**
> 4. **One insert level only** (no `a.1` or `.25a`)
> 5. **Filename is the source of truth, folder is optional**
> 
> Follow these and this system will survive:
> - Supplements
> - Emergency filings
> - Appeals
> - Counsel takeover
>

> - **0002** → Exhibit B
>

> ## 2️⃣ COPY-PASTE POWERSHELL SCRIPT (WINDOWS)
> 
> This will **create everything above instantly**.
> 
> ### How to use
> 1. Open PowerShell  
> 2. `cd` to where you want the case folder  
> 3. Paste **everything** below  
> 4. Press Enter  
> 
> ---
> 
> ```powershell
> $root = "FCFCU-49D03-2501-MF-002559"
> 
> $structure = @{
>     "A_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW" = @(
>         "A0.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "A0.00.010_MASTER_CASE_INDEX.md",
>         "A0.01.001_ONE_PAGE_CASE_SUMMARY.md",
>         "A0.01.002_HEARING_SCOPE_AND_RELIEF.md"
>     )
>     "B_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW" = @(
>         "B1.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "B1.01.001_CORE_ISSUE_STATEMENT.md",
>         "B1.01.002_TRIAL_RULE_4_1_B_STANDARD.md",
>         "B1.01.003_VOID_VS_VOIDABLE_CASE_LAW.md"
>     )
>     "C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS" = @(
>         "C2.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "C2.01.001_MOTION_TO_VACATE_VOID_JUDGMENT.md",
>         "C2.02.001_EMERGENCY_MOTION_STAY_OR_QUASH.md",
>         "C2.03.001_SUPPLEMENTAL_EMERGENCY_MOTION.md",
>         "C2.04.001_PROPOSED_ORDER_VACATE.md",
>         "C2.04.002_PROPOSED_ORDER_STAY_WRIT.md"
>     )
>     "D_DELIVERY_SERVICE" = @(
>         "D3.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "D3.01.001_SUMMONS_INCOMPLETE.pdf",
>         "D3.02.001_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-03-05.pdf",
>         "D3.02.002_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-04-15.pdf",
>         "D3.03.001_SERVICE_DEFECT_ANALYSIS.md"
>     )
>     "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN" = @(
>         "E4.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "E4.01.001_DEFAULT_JUDGMENT_ENTRY.pdf",
>         "E4.02.001_PETITION_FOR_WRIT_OF_ASSISTANCE.pdf",
>         "E4.03.001_WRIT_OF_ASSISTANCE_ISSUED.pdf",
>         "E4.04.001_REMOVAL_ENFORCEMENT_RECORD.pdf",
>         "E4.05.001_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN_SUMMARY.md"
>     )
>     "F_FACTS_DECLARATIONS" = @(
>         "F5.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "F5.01.001_AFFIDAVIT_NOT_SERVED.md",
>         "F5.02.001_DECLARATION_ONGOING_HARM.md",
>         "F5.03.001_CREDIBILITY_DECLARATION.md"
>     )
>     "G_GROUNDS_ADA" = @(
>         "G6.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "G6.01.001_ADA_NOTICE.pdf",
>         "G6.02.001_ADA_SUPPORTING_DOCUMENTATION.pdf",
>         "G6.03.001_ADA_IMPACT_SUMMARY.md"
>     )
>     "H_HARD_EXHIBITS" = @(
>         "H7.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "H7.01.0001_EXHIBIT_A_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-03-05.pdf",
>         "H7.01.0002_EXHIBIT_B_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-04-15.pdf",
>         "H7.01.0003_EXHIBIT_C_INCOMPLETE_SUMMONS.pdf",
>         "H7.01.0004_EXHIBIT_D_DEFAULT_JUDGMENT_MOTION.pdf",
>         "H7.01.0005_EXHIBIT_E_PETITION_FOR_WRIT.pdf",
>         "H7.01.0006_EXHIBIT_F_AFFIDAVIT.pdf",
>         "H7.01.0007_EXHIBIT_G1_ADA_NOTICE.pdf",
>         "H7.01.0008_EXHIBIT_G2_AES_ADA_DOCUMENTS.pdf"
>     )
>     "I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE" = @(
>         "I8.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>         "I8.01.001_FULL_DOCKET.pdf",
>         "I8.02.001_RESEARCH_AND_NOTES.md",
>         "I8.99.999_INTERNAL_DO_NOT_PRINT.md"
>     )
> }
> 
> New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $root -Force | Out-Null
> 
> foreach ($folder in $structure.Keys) {
>     $folderPath = Join-Path $root $folder
>     New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $folderPath -Force | Out-Null
> 
>     foreach ($file in $structure[$folder]) {
>         $filePath = Join-Path $folderPath $file
>         if (-not (Test-Path $filePath)) {
>             New-Item -ItemType File -Path $filePath | Out-Null
>         }
>     }
> }
> 
> Write-Host "Case binder structure created successfully."
> ```
>

> ## 2) UPDATED POWERSHELL SCRIPT (CREATES ALL FOLDERS + PLACEHOLDERS)
> 
> Copy/paste into PowerShell **from the directory where you want the case folder created**.
> 
> ```powershell
> $root = "FCFCU-49D03-2501-MF-002559"
> 
> $foldersAndFiles = @{
>   "A_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW\A0_00_COVER_INDEX" = @(
>     "A0.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md",
>     "A0.00.010_MASTER_CASE_INDEX.md"
>   )
>   "A_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW\A0_01_OVERVIEW" = @(
>     "A0.01.001_ONE_PAGE_CASE_SUMMARY.md",
>     "A0.01.002_HEARING_SCOPE_AND_RELIEF.md"
>   )
> 
>   "B_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW\B1_00_COVER" = @("B1.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "B_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW\B1_01_ISSUE_LAW" = @(
>     "B1.01.001_CORE_ISSUE_STATEMENT.md",
>     "B1.01.002_TRIAL_RULE_4_1_B_STANDARD.md",
>     "B1.01.003_VOID_VS_VOIDABLE_CASE_LAW.md"
>   )
> 
>   "C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS\C2_00_COVER" = @("C2.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS\C2_01_MOTION_VACATE" = @("C2.01.001_MOTION_TO_VACATE_VOID_JUDGMENT.md")
>   "C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS\C2_02_EMERGENCY_STAY_QUASH" = @("C2.02.001_EMERGENCY_MOTION_STAY_OR_QUASH.md")
>   "C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS\C2_03_SUPPLEMENTAL" = @("C2.03.001_SUPPLEMENTAL_EMERGENCY_MOTION.md")
>   "C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS\C2_04_PROPOSED_ORDERS" = @(
>     "C2.04.001_PROPOSED_ORDER_VACATE.md",
>     "C2.04.002_PROPOSED_ORDER_STAY_WRIT.md"
>   )
> 
>   "D_DELIVERY_SERVICE\D3_00_COVER" = @("D3.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "D_DELIVERY_SERVICE\D3_01_SUMMONS" = @("D3.01.001_SUMMONS_INCOMPLETE.pdf")
>   "D_DELIVERY_SERVICE\D3_02_SHERIFF_RETURNS" = @(
>     "D3.02.001_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-03-05.pdf",
>     "D3.02.002_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-04-15.pdf"
>   )
>   "D_DELIVERY_SERVICE\D3_03_SERVICE_ANALYSIS" = @("D3.03.001_SERVICE_DEFECT_ANALYSIS.md")
> 
>   "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN\E4_00_COVER" = @("E4.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN\E4_01_DEFAULT_JUDGMENT" = @("E4.01.001_DEFAULT_JUDGMENT_ENTRY.pdf")
>   "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN\E4_02_PETITION_FOR_WRIT" = @("E4.02.001_PETITION_FOR_WRIT_OF_ASSISTANCE.pdf")
>   "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN\E4_03_WRIT_ISSUED" = @("E4.03.001_WRIT_OF_ASSISTANCE_ISSUED.pdf")
>   "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN\E4_04_REMOVAL_ENFORCEMENT" = @("E4.04.001_REMOVAL_ENFORCEMENT_RECORD.pdf")
>   "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN\E4_05_CHAIN_SUMMARY" = @("E4.05.001_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN_SUMMARY.md")
> 
>   "F_FACTS_DECLARATIONS\F5_00_COVER" = @("F5.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "F_FACTS_DECLARATIONS\F5_01_AFFIDAVIT_NOT_SERVED" = @("F5.01.001_AFFIDAVIT_NOT_SERVED.md")
>   "F_FACTS_DECLARATIONS\F5_02_DECLARATION_ONGOING_HARM" = @("F5.02.001_DECLARATION_ONGOING_HARM.md")
>   "F_FACTS_DECLARATIONS\F5_03_CREDIBILITY_DECLARATION" = @("F5.03.001_CREDIBILITY_DECLARATION.md")
> 
>   "G_GROUNDS_ADA\G6_00_COVER" = @("G6.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "G_GROUNDS_ADA\G6_01_ADA_NOTICE" = @("G6.01.001_ADA_NOTICE.pdf")
>   "G_GROUNDS_ADA\G6_02_ADA_SUPPORTING" = @("G6.02.001_ADA_SUPPORTING_DOCUMENTATION.pdf")
>   "G_GROUNDS_ADA\G6_03_ADA_IMPACT_SUMMARY" = @("G6.03.001_ADA_IMPACT_SUMMARY.md")
> 
>   "H_HARD_EXHIBITS\H7_00_COVER" = @("H7.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "H_HARD_EXHIBITS\H7_01_EXHIBITS_A_G" = @(
>     "H7.01.0001_EXHIBIT_A_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-03-05.pdf",
>     "H7.01.0002_EXHIBIT_B_SHERIFF_RETURN_2025-04-15.pdf",
>     "H7.01.0003_EXHIBIT_C_INCOMPLETE_SUMMONS.pdf",
>     "H7.01.0004_EXHIBIT_D_DEFAULT_JUDGMENT_MOTION.pdf",
>     "H7.01.0005_EXHIBIT_E_PETITION_FOR_WRIT.pdf",
>     "H7.01.0006_EXHIBIT_F_AFFIDAVIT.pdf",
>     "H7.01.0007_EXHIBIT_G1_ADA_NOTICE.pdf",
>     "H7.01.0008_EXHIBIT_G2_AES_ADA_DOCUMENTS.pdf"
>   )
> 
>   "I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\I8_00_COVER" = @("I8.00.000_SECTION_COVER.md")
>   "I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\I8_01_FULL_DOCKET" = @("I8.01.001_FULL_DOCKET.pdf")
>   "I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\I8_02_RESEARCH_NOTES" = @("I8.02.001_RESEARCH_AND_NOTES.md")
>   "I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\I8_99_DO_NOT_PRINT" = @("I8.99.999_INTERNAL_DO_NOT_PRINT.md")
> 
>   "09_EXPORTS\COURT_SET" = @()
>   "09_EXPORTS\PERSONAL_MASTER" = @()
>   "09_EXPORTS\ARCHIVE" = @()
> }
> 
> # Create root
> New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $root -Force | Out-Null
> 
> # Create all folders/files
> foreach ($relFolder in $foldersAndFiles.Keys) {
>   $folderPath = Join-Path $root $relFolder
>   New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $folderPath -Force | Out-Null
> 
>   foreach ($file in $foldersAndFiles[$relFolder]) {
>     $filePath = Join-Path $folderPath $file
>     if (-not (Test-Path $filePath)) {
>       New-Item -ItemType File -Path $filePath | Out-Null
>     }
>   }
> }
> 
> # Add _README.md in each top-level tab folder
> $topTabs = @(
>   "A_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW",
>   "B_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW",
>   "C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS",
>   "D_DELIVERY_SERVICE",
>   "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN",
>   "F_FACTS_DECLARATIONS",
>   "G_GROUNDS_ADA",
>   "H_HARD_EXHIBITS",
>   "I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE"
> )
> 
> foreach ($tab in $topTabs) {
>   $readme = Join-Path (Join-Path $root $tab) "_README.md"
>   if (-not (Test-Path $readme)) { New-Item -ItemType File -Path $readme | Out-Null }
> }
> 
> Write-Host "Done: Created binder repo structure with subsection folders + placeholders."
> ```

### Assistant
> Short answer: **no — and that’s intentional and correct**.
> 
> What you’ve built *so far* is the **COURT-SAFE BINDER TRACK**.  
> What you’re asking about now is the **WORKSPACE / WAR ROOM TRACK**.
> 
> If we mix them, you will:
> - confuse print vs think
> - risk handing the wrong thing up
> - overload your ADHD under pressure
> - destroy the elegance of the binder
> 
> So we solve this by **explicitly splitting the universe into TWO PARALLEL TRACKS** that are linked, not merged.
> 
> This is the missing piece.
> 
> ---
> 
> # THE TWO-TRACK SYSTEM (LOCK THIS CONCEPT)
> 
> ## TRACK 1 — **COURT BINDER (WHAT WE JUST BUILT)**
> **Purpose:**  
> - Printed
> - Handed up
> - Judge-facing
> - Immutable once filed
> 
> **Location (already built):**
> ```
> FCFCU-49D03-2501-MF-002559/
> ```
> 
> Rules:
> - Clean
> - Minimal
> - No brainstorming
> - No feelings
> - No speculation
> - No PR
> - No drafts
> - No trackers
> 
> This is a **presentation artifact**, not a brain.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## TRACK 2 — **CASE WAR ROOM (YOUR BRAIN)**
> **Purpose:**  
> - Thinking
> - Strategy
> - Evidence intake
> - Drafting
> - Advocacy
> - Parallel complaints
> - Media
> - Healing + narrative
> 
> This lives **outside** the binder root.
> 
> ---

> # FINAL, CORRECT TOP-LEVEL LAYOUT
> 
> Put both under a single parent so your brain sees the whole system:
>

> 
> You **never print directly** from `02_WAR_ROOM`.  
> You **only promote** things into `01_COURT_BINDER`.
> 
> This is the key ADHD safety rail.

>

>

> - Draft → reviewed → finalized → **copied into COURT_BINDER**
> - Evidence → validated → labeled → **renamed and copied**
> - Strategy → distilled → **1-page summary only** promoted

> - Binder stays calm and finite
> - War Room absorbs chaos safely
> - You can think freely without court risk
> - Printing becomes mechanical, not emotional

### User

### Assistant
> Yes. This is the **correct unifying move**, and you’re thinking about this exactly the right way.
> 
> What we will do is:
> 
> - **Mirror the COURT BINDER A–I structure exactly**
> - Prefix **everything in the War Room with `W`**
> - Keep **section letters, subsection numbers, and semantics identical**
> - Allow **direct promotion** (copy + drop `W`) without renaming logic
> - Preserve ADHD mental alignment under stress
> 
> This gives you **structural isomorphism**: same map, different risk level.
> 
> Below is the **LOCKED WAR ROOM SPEC**.
> 
> ---
> 
> # WAR ROOM NUMBERING & PREFIX RULE (LOCKED)
> 
> **Rule 1 — Prefix**
> - Every War Room folder/file starts with **`W`**
> - Court Binder uses **no prefix**
> 
> **Rule 2 — Same Tabs, Same Meaning**
> - WA ↔ A (Anchor)
> - WB ↔ B (Basis)
> - WC ↔ C (Claims)
> - WD ↔ D (Delivery)
> - WE ↔ E (Effects)
> - WF ↔ F (Facts)
> - WG ↔ G (Grounds)
> - WH ↔ H (Exhibits / Evidence)
> - WI ↔ I (Internal / Reference)
> 
> **Rule 3 — Promotion**
> - Promotion = **copy file → remove leading `W` → place in Binder**
> - No renumbering
> - No reinterpretation
> - No mental translation
>

> │   │   └── WH7.01.0002_POTENTIAL_EXHIBIT_B.pdf
> │   └── _README.md
> │
> ├── WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/
> │   ├── WI8_00_DOCKET_RECORD/
> │   │   ├── WI8.00.001_FULL_DOCKET.pdf
> │   │   └── WI8.00.002_DOCKET_NOTES.md
> │   ├── WI8_01_PUBLIC_ADVOCACY/
> │   │   ├── WI8.01.001_PRESS_STRATEGY.md
> │   │   ├── WI8.01.002_SOCIAL_MEDIA_PLAN.md
> │   │   └── WI8.01.003_TIMING_AND_RISK.md
> │   ├── WI8_02_DAMAGES_AND_SETTLEMENT/
> │   │   ├── WI8.02.001_ECONOMIC_HARM.md
> │   │   ├── WI8.02.002_NON_ECONOMIC_HARM.md
> │   │   └── WI8.02.003_SETTLEMENT_SCENARIOS.md
> │   └── _README.md
> │
> └── WZ_PROMOTION_PIPELINE/
>     ├── WZ9.00.001_READY_FOR_BINDER.md
>     ├── WZ9.00.002_REJECTED_FOR_COURT.md
>     └── WZ9.00.003_PROMOTION_LOG.md
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> # WHY THIS IS THE RIGHT DESIGN (NO FLUFF)
> 
> - Your **mental map stays constant**
> - Every idea already “knows” where it *would* land in court
> - Promotion is frictionless
> - You never ask “where does this go?”
> - You can safely explore aggressive strategies without contaminating the binder
> - Obsidian backlinks remain meaningful across tracks
> 
> This is **how high-end litigation teams actually work**, just formalized for a solo operator with ADHD.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## NEXT STEP (WE DO THIS CLEANLY)
> 
> Say one of the following **exactly**:
> 
> - **“BUILD WAR ROOM SCRIPT”** → I generate the PowerShell script to create all of this  
> - **“PROMOTION CHECKLIST”** → 1-page rules for when/how a `W*` file becomes court-safe  
> - **“OBSIDIAN TEMPLATES”** → auto-prefilled note templates per section (WA, WB, etc.)
> 
> We proceed one step at a time and lock each layer.

### User
> GIVE ME EVERYTHING THE SCRIPT TO BUILD THE COURT BINDER DIRECTORY, WAR ROOM DIRECTORY, PROMOTION CHECKLIST, AND OBSIDIAN TEMPLATES. THEN WE CAN WORK ON MAPPING AND FILLING UP THIS DIGITAL BINDER(S) SO I CAN GO PRINT IN THE COMING DAYS, WE WILL COLOR CODE THEM, WHITE IS FOR THE JUDGE, BLUE IS MYPERSONAL COPY, A BROWN COPY FOR THE OPPOSITION AND A RED BINDER WITH EVERYTHING RED FOR DONT ACCIDENTLY LET NOBODY SEE THIS INTERNAL ONLY, COURT AND WARROOM AND ARCHVIE.

### Assistant
> Understood. Here is the **full package** in one place:
> 
> 1) **One PowerShell script** that builds **both**: Court Binder + War Room + Archive + Templates folder  
> 2) **Promotion Checklist** (dummy-proof)  
> 3) **Obsidian Templates** (drop-in ready)  
> 4) **Color-coded print/binder system** (white/blue/brown/red) mapped to outputs and rules
> 
> Everything below is designed so you can run it once and immediately start mapping/filling.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 1) POWERHELL: BUILD EVERYTHING (COURT + WAR ROOM + ARCHIVE + TEMPLATES)
> 
> **How to run**
> - Open PowerShell
> - `cd` to the folder where you want `FCFCU_CASE` created
> - Paste entire script, press Enter
> 
> ```powershell
> # ================================
> # FCFCU_CASE Builder (Court + War Room + Archive + Obsidian Templates)
> # ================================
> 
> $caseRoot = "FCFCU_CASE"
> $courtRoot = Join-Path $caseRoot "01_COURT_BINDER\FCFCU-49D03-2501-MF-002559"
> $warRoot   = Join-Path $caseRoot "02_WAR_ROOM"
> $archRoot  = Join-Path $caseRoot "99_ARCHIVE"
> 
> # ---------- Helpers ----------
> function Ensure-Dir($path) {
>   New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $path -Force | Out-Null
> }
> 
> function Ensure-File($path, $content = "") {
>   if (-not (Test-Path $path)) {
>     $parent = Split-Path $path -Parent
>     Ensure-Dir $parent
>     Set-Content -Path $path -Value $content -Encoding UTF8
>   }
> }
> 
> # ---------- Create base roots ----------
> Ensure-Dir $caseRoot
> Ensure-Dir $courtRoot
> Ensure-Dir $warRoot
> Ensure-Dir $archRoot
> 
> # ---------- Court Binder (A–I) with subsection folders ----------

> 
> ## 2) PROMOTION CHECKLIST (DUMMY-PROOF, COURT-SAFE)
> Copy this into:
> - `FCFCU_CASE/PROMOTION_CHECKLIST.md` **and**
> - `FCFCU_CASE/02_WAR_ROOM/WZ_PROMOTION_PIPELINE/WZ9.00.010_PROMOTION_CHECKLIST.md`
> 
> ```markdown
> # Promotion Checklist (War Room → Court Binder)
> Status: LOCKED PROCEDURE
> 
> ## Definitions
> - **War Room file:** starts with `W` (e.g., `WD3...`, `WH7...`)
> - **Court Binder file:** identical code WITHOUT `W` (e.g., `D3...`, `H7...`)
> - **Promotion:** copy the finalized item into Court Binder and remove `W`.
> 
> ## Rule 0 — Safety
> If it contains ANY of:
> - strategy speculation
> - media/PR
> - settlement posture not filed
> - personal narrative
> - mental health / private life details
> - accusations not supported by exhibits
> → it **stays War Room** (internal/red only).
> 
> ## Rule 1 — Court relevance
> To promote, it must answer one of:
> - What is the legal issue?
> - What relief am I requesting?
> - What admissible fact supports it?
> - What docket item proves it?
> 
> If it doesn’t serve a hearing purpose, it stays War Room.
> 
> ## Rule 2 — Evidence hygiene (for PDFs / images)
> Before promoting to Court Binder:
> - file name is correct code (A–I section) and date is correct
> - no extra pages or unrelated material included
> - legible at 100% zoom and printed
> - if highlights/annotations exist, preserve an unmarked original in War Room
> 
> ## Rule 3 — Sleeve rule (physical handling)
> Promote-to-binder items that should be **sleeved**:
> - exhibits (Tab H) ALWAYS
> - court orders / writs / returns (Tabs D/E) YES
> - anything you may hand up YES
> 
> Anything that is your narrative or summary: NO sleeve (hole-punch).
> 
> ## Rule 4 — Header rule (every promoted MD)
> Top of every Court Binder markdown must include:
> - the code (e.g., `D3.03.001`)
> - the title
> - “Purpose” (1 sentence)
> - “Ask/Use” (what you will say while pointing at it)
> 
> ## Rule 5 — Copy procedure (no data loss)
> 1. COPY the War Room file into the correct Court Binder folder
> 2. REMOVE leading `W` from the filename only
> 3. DO NOT change numbering
> 4. Update the relevant Export Master note to include it
> 
> ## Rule 6 — Logging
> Record promotions in:
> - `WZ9.00.003_PROMOTION_LOG.md`
> Include:
> - date
> - from (war path)
> - to (binder path)
> - reason (1 line)
> 
> ## Rule 7 — Print sets
> Only print from the Export Masters:
> - `COURT_SET_MASTER` (White)
> - `PERSONAL_MASTER` (Blue)
> - `OPPOSITION_SET_MASTER` (Brown)
> - `INTERNAL_RED_MASTER` (Red)
> Never print straight from War Room unless it’s for internal planning.
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 3) OBSIDIAN TEMPLATES (DROP-IN READY)
> 
> Put these files in `FCFCU_CASE/03_OBSIDIAN_TEMPLATES/` and set Obsidian Templates plugin to that folder.
> 
> ### A) `TEMPLATE_SECTION_COVER.md`
> ```markdown
> ---
> type: section_cover
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: {{TAB}}
> print: true
> sleeve: false
> ---
> 
> # {{CODE}} — {{TAB}} (Section Cover)
> 
> **Purpose:**  
> - 
> 
> **What the court should understand from this tab:**  
> - 
> - 
> 
> **What I’m asking for (if applicable):**  
> - 
> ```
> 
> ### B) `TEMPLATE_SECTION_INDEX.md`
> ```markdown
> ---
> type: section_index
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: {{TAB}}
> print: true
> sleeve: false
> ---
> 
> # {{CODE}} — {{TAB}} (Index)
> 
> ## Contents (in order)
> 1. 
> 2. 
> 3. 
> 
> ## Use in court (script)
> - “Your Honor, this tab shows…”
> - “The key document is…”
> ```
> 
> ### C) `TEMPLATE_COURT_DOC.md`
> ```markdown
> ---
> type: court_doc
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: {{TAB}}
> print: true
> sleeve: {{SLEEVE}}
> ---
> 
> # {{CODE}} — {{TITLE}}
> 
> **Purpose (1 sentence):**  
> -
> 
> **Use in court (what I will say):**  
> -
> 
> **Key points (bullets):**
> - 
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Cross-references:**
> - Related exhibit(s): 
> - Related docket item(s):
> ```
> 
> ### D) `TEMPLATE_WAR_NOTE.md`
> ```markdown
> ---
> type: war_note
> code: {{WCODE}}
> tab: {{WTAB}}
> print: false
> internal: true
> ---
> 
> # {{WCODE}} — {{TITLE}} (WAR ROOM)
> 
> **Working hypothesis / goal:**  
> -
> 
> **Evidence to validate:**  
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Risks / pushback:**  
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Promotion candidate?**
> - [ ] Yes
> - [ ] No
> If yes, target court slot: `{{TARGET_CODE}}`
> ```
> 
> ### E) `TEMPLATE_EXHIBIT_LABEL.md`
> ```markdown
> ---
> type: exhibit_label
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: H_HARD_EXHIBITS
> print: true
> sleeve: true
> ---
> 
> # {{CODE}} — EXHIBIT {{LETTER}}: {{TITLE}}
> 
> **Source:**  
> - 
> 
> **What it proves (1 line):**  
> -
> 
> **Notes for court handling:**
> - Keep in sleeve
> - Hand-up ready
> ```
> 
> ### F) `TEMPLATE_HANDUP_PACKET_NOTE.md`
> ```markdown
> ---
> type: handup_packet
> print: true
> sleeve: true
> ---
> 
> # HAND-UP PACKET — {{PACKET_NAME}}
> 
> **When to hand up:**  
> -
> 
> **Contains (exact):**
> - 
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Instructions:**
> - Provide to judge only upon request or at the moment referenced.
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> ## 4) COLOR-CODED BINDERS + PRINT SETS (WHITE / BLUE / BROWN / RED)
> 
> This is the **operational rule** so you don’t accidentally leak internal material.
> 
> ### WHITE (Judge) — “Court Set”
> - Print only from:  
>   `01_COURT_BINDER/.../09_EXPORTS/COURT_SET/00_COURT_SET_MASTER.md`
> - Contents: only Court Binder Tabs **A–H** (never I unless you know what you’re doing)
> - Sleeves: exhibits + official records as specified
> 
> ### BLUE (Your personal, court-ready) — “Personal Master”
> - Print only from:  
>   `.../09_EXPORTS/PERSONAL_MASTER/00_PERSONAL_MASTER.md`
> - Can include Tab I if you want, but keep I at back and flagged “INTERNAL”
> 
> ### BROWN (Opposition) — “Opposition Set”
> - Print only from:  
>   `.../09_EXPORTS/OPPOSITION_SET/00_OPPOSITION_SET_MASTER.md`
> - Rule: **no internal notes, no strategy, no war room, no narrative**
> - Typically: tabs A–H, but possibly reduced (we’ll curate later)
> 
> ### RED (Internal Only) — “Internal Red Master”
> - Print only from:  
>   `.../09_EXPORTS/INTERNAL_RED_SET/00_INTERNAL_RED_MASTER.md`
> - This can include War Room extracts if you insist, but label every page:
>   **INTERNAL – DO NOT DISCLOSE**
> 
> **Hard rule:** Red binder never leaves your control.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## What you do next (in this order)
> 1) Run the script → confirm the folders exist  
> 2) Point Obsidian at `FCFCU_CASE` as a vault (or add as a vault folder)  
> 3) Set Templates folder to `FCFCU_CASE/03_OBSIDIAN_TEMPLATES`  
> 4) Then we create your first export masters:
>    - Court (white)
>    - Personal (blue)
>    - Opposition (brown)
>    - Red (internal)
> 
> If you reply **“BUILD EXPORT MASTERS NOW”**, I will generate the exact starter content for the four `00_*_MASTER.md` files, in the correct print order, with embed lines ready to paste.

> ``` WE MUST KEEP  ALOG OF MOVES AND CHANGE TO HIT UNDUE IF WE HAVE TO, THE MIGRATION SHOULD BE MOVING TO CORRECT LOCATION AND CORRECT NAMING I THINK OUR BEST MOVE IS SIMPLY LEAVING CURRENT NAMES JUST ADDING THE CORRECT NUMBERED PREFIX FOR CONTINUITY.

### Assistant
> Good. You’re thinking correctly: **migration must be reversible and auditable** (undue influence / chain-of-custody / credibility). And yes: **best move is “keep original names” + “prepend new ordered prefix”** so nothing looks like you’re rewriting history.
> 
> Below is the complete migration spec:
> 
> 1) **Authoritative mapping**: legacy → new location (Court Binder vs War Room vs Archive)  
> 2) **Rename policy**: “prefix only, never rewrite”  
> 3) **Move log requirements** (CSV + hash option)  
> 4) **PowerShell migration script** that:
>    - copies (or moves—your choice) legacy into new structure
>    - adds prefixes
>    - writes a move log
>    - optionally computes SHA256 hashes for evidence-grade auditability
> 
> ---
> 
> # 0) NON-NEGOTIABLE MIGRATION RULES (UNDUE-INFLUENCE SAFE)
> 
> ## Rule A — Do NOT overwrite originals
> - Migration should be **COPY-first**.
> - Keep `__legacy` intact until after hearing.
> - If you need to “clean up” later, do it after the hearing, and keep logs.
> 
> ## Rule B — Rename policy: PREFIX ONLY
> - New name = `NEWPREFIX__` + `OldName`
> - Example:
>   - `Case_Log.md` → `WI8.02.010__Case_Log.md`
>   - `2025-12-10_MTV_Exhibits_Combined.pdf` → `WH7.01.0100__2025-12-10_MTV_Exhibits_Combined.pdf`
> 
> ## Rule C — Log every operation
> Every copied/renamed file gets a row:
> - timestamp
> - action (COPY or MOVE)
> - src path
> - dst path
> - old name
> - new name
> - sha256 (optional but recommended for PDFs/images/videos)
> - notes (mapping rule used)
> 
> This is your “chain-of-changes” defense.
> 
> ---
> 
> # 1) LEGACY → NEW STRUCTURE MAPPING (AUTHORITATIVE)
> 
> Your new universe is:
> - `01_COURT_BINDER/FCFCU-.../` (court-facing clean binder)
> - `02_WAR_ROOM/` (everything else, prefixed W)
> - `99_ARCHIVE/` (legacy preserved snapshots, exports, stale)
> 
> ### A) `__legacy/00_admin/00_trackers/`
> **Destination:** War Room `WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE` (because trackers are internal ops)
> - `Case_Log.md`, session summaries, conversation logs, expenses, financial trackers:
>   - → `02_WAR_ROOM/WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/WI8_02_DAMAGES_AND_SETTLEMENT/`
>   - Prefix suggestion: `WI8.02.01x__*`
> 
> ### B) `__legacy/00_admin/05_timeline/`
> **Destination:** War Room `WA_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW` (timeline is command/control)
> - → `02_WAR_ROOM/WA_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW/WA0_00_COMMAND_MAP/` **and** optionally `WA0_01_HEARING_PLANNING/`
> - Prefix suggestion: `WA0.00.03x__*` (timeline artifacts)
> 
> ### C) `__legacy/00_admin/10_overviews/`
> **Destination:** War Room `WE_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN` (overviews/one-pagers/visual chain)
> - → `02_WAR_ROOM/WE_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN/WE4_00_CHAIN_ANALYSIS/`
> - Prefix: `WE4.00.01x__*`
> 
> ### D) `__legacy/00_admin/20_strategy/`
> **Destination:** War Room `WB` and `WE` depending on content
> - ADA Title II → `WG_GROUNDS_ADA/WG6_00_ADA_STRATEGY/`
> - Jurisdiction/service TR 4.1(B) → `WB_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW/WB1_00_LAW_RESEARCH/`
> - Void vs voidable TR60(B) → `WB.../WB1_00_LAW_RESEARCH/`
> - Strategic canvases → `WA.../WA0_00_COMMAND_MAP/`
> - Prefix: `WG6.00.01x__`, `WB1.00.01x__`, `WA0.00.01x__`
> 
> ### E) `__legacy/00_admin/30_drafts-templates/`
> **Destination:** War Room drafts (never court binder directly)
> - Motions drafts → `02_WAR_ROOM/WC_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS/WC2_00_DRAFT_MOTIONS/`
> - Declarations/affidavits → `02_WAR_ROOM/WF_FACTS_DECLARATIONS/WF5_01_DRAFT_DECLARATIONS/`
> - Exhibits list templates → `02_WAR_ROOM/WH_HARD_EVIDENCE/WH7_01_POTENTIAL_EXHIBITS/` (or keep in templates)
> - Proposed orders → `02_WAR_ROOM/WC.../WC2_01_PROPOSED_ORDERS/`
> - Prefix: `WC2.00.01x__`, `WF5.01.01x__`, `WC2.01.01x__`
> 
> ### F) `__legacy/00_admin/40_action_center/`
> **Destination:** War Room hearing planning
> - decision tree / pre-hearing checklist → `02_WAR_ROOM/WA_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW/WA0_01_HEARING_PLANNING/`
> - Prefix: `WA0.01.01x__`
> 
> ### G) `__legacy/00_admin/Contacts.md` and `Talking_Points.md`
> **Destination:** War Room hearing planning (and later promote a cleaned version)
> - → `02_WAR_ROOM/WA.../WA0_01_HEARING_PLANNING/`
> - Prefix: `WA0.01.02x__`
> 
> ### H) `__legacy/10_filings/`
> **Destination:** Court Binder primary source PDFs
> - Filed motions PDFs (01_motion_vacate.pdf etc.) → `01_COURT_BINDER/.../C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS/...` as source artifacts or `09_EXPORTS/ARCHIVE/` if you keep “filed packets” separate.
> - Filed receipts → `01_COURT_BINDER/.../I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/I8_99_DO_NOT_PRINT/` (or `09_EXPORTS/ARCHIVE/`)
> - Draft docx stay in War Room drafts.
> 
> ### I) `__legacy/20_evidence_vault/`
> **Destination:** War Room evidence intake + Court Binder exhibits (promoted copies)
> - RAW photos/video/receipts → `02_WAR_ROOM/WH_HARD_EVIDENCE/WH7_00_RAW_INTAKE/`
> - Exhibit sets A–H initial → `02_WAR_ROOM/WH.../WH7_01_POTENTIAL_EXHIBITS/`
> - Then when final: copy promoted into Court Binder Tab H (`H7...`) without the W.
> 
> ### J) `__legacy/30_court_record/10_docket/`
> **Destination:** War Room docket record (and optionally a single “Full docket” in Court Binder Tab I)
> - → `02_WAR_ROOM/WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/WI8_00_DOCKET_RECORD/`
> - Prefix: `WI8.00.00x__` keeping original numbering.
> 
> ### K) `__legacy/personal_narrative/`
> **Destination:** War Room internal reference / public advocacy depending on subfolder
> - Public narrative → `02_WAR_ROOM/WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/WI8_01_PUBLIC_ADVOCACY/`
> - Exposure/harm → `02_WAR_ROOM/WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/WI8_02_DAMAGES_AND_SETTLEMENT/`
> - Internal analysis/premonitions → `02_WAR_ROOM/WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/WI8_99_INTERNAL_ONLY/` (we will create this folder)
> - Donations → `02_WAR_ROOM/WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/WI8_01_PUBLIC_ADVOCACY/`
> 
> ### L) `__legacy/tools/`
> **Destination:** `99_ARCHIVE/tools_legacy/` (keep intact)
> - You do not want tooling intermingled with binder content right now.
> 
> ---
> 
> # 2) MIGRATION LOG FILES (CREATE THESE)
> 
> In `FCFCU_CASE/` create:
> 
> - `MIGRATION_LOG.csv` (every operation, append-only)
> - `MIGRATION_NOTES.md` (why decisions were made, high level)
> 
> CSV columns:
> ```
> timestamp,action,src,dst,old_name,new_name,sha256,rule
> ```
> 
> ---
> 
> # 3) POWERSHELL: COPY + PREFIX + LOG (AUDIT-SAFE)
> 
> **What this does**
> - Copies from your existing `__legacy` into `FCFCU_CASE/02_WAR_ROOM` and `01_COURT_BINDER` targets
> - Adds prefix-only naming
> - Logs everything
> - Optionally hashes files (recommended)
> 
> **Before running**
> - Put this script somewhere safe (like `FCFCU_CASE/tools/`)
> - Update `$legacyPath` to where your actual `__legacy` folder is.
> 
> ```powershell
> # ==========================================
> # FCFCU Legacy Migration (COPY + PREFIX + LOG)
> # ==========================================
> 
> param(
>   [string]$legacyPath = ".\__legacy",
>   [string]$caseRoot   = ".\FCFCU_CASE",
>   [ValidateSet("COPY","MOVE")] [string]$mode = "COPY",
>   [bool]$hash = $true
> )
> 
> function Ensure-Dir($p){ New-Item -ItemType Directory -Force -Path $p | Out-Null }
> function NowIso(){ (Get-Date).ToString("yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss") }
> 
> $logPath = Join-Path $caseRoot "MIGRATION_LOG.csv"
> Ensure-Dir $caseRoot
> if (-not (Test-Path $logPath)) {
>   "timestamp,action,src,dst,old_name,new_name,sha256,rule" | Out-File $logPath -Encoding UTF8
> }
> 
> function Sha256($p){
>   if (-not $hash) { return "" }
>   if (-not (Test-Path $p)) { return "" }
>   try { return (Get-FileHash -Algorithm SHA256 -Path $p).Hash } catch { return "" }
> }
> 
> function LogRow($action,$src,$dst,$old,$new,$h,$rule){
>   $line = "{0},{1},""{2}"",""{3}"",""{4}"",""{5}"",{6},""{7}""" -f (NowIso),$action,$src,$dst,$old,$new,$h,$rule
>   Add-Content -Path $logPath -Value $line -Encoding UTF8
> }
> 
> function CopyOrMove($src,$dst,$rule){
>   Ensure-Dir (Split-Path $dst -Parent)
>   $old = Split-Path $src -Leaf
>   $new = Split-Path $dst -Leaf
> 
>   if ($mode -eq "MOVE") {
>     Move-Item -LiteralPath $src -Destination $dst -Force
>     $h = Sha256 $dst
>     LogRow "MOVE" $src $dst $old $new $h $rule
>   } else {
>     Copy-Item -LiteralPath $src -Destination $dst -Force
>     $h = Sha256 $dst
>     LogRow "COPY" $src $dst $old $new $h $rule
>   }
> }
> 
> # ---- Define destinations
> $courtRoot = Join-Path $caseRoot "01_COURT_BINDER\FCFCU-49D03-2501-MF-002559"
> $warRoot   = Join-Path $caseRoot "02_WAR_ROOM"
> $archRoot  = Join-Path $caseRoot "99_ARCHIVE"
> 
> Ensure-Dir $courtRoot
> Ensure-Dir $warRoot
> Ensure-Dir $archRoot
> 
> # Create extra internal-only war folder for narrative/internal analysis
> Ensure-Dir (Join-Path $warRoot "WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_99_INTERNAL_ONLY")
> 
> # ---- Mapping rules: legacy subpaths -> (dest folder, prefix)
> # Keep it simple and auditable: prefix-only; keep original filename after "__"
> $map = @(
>   @{ src="00_admin\00_trackers"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_02_DAMAGES_AND_SETTLEMENT"; prefix="WI8.02.010"; rule="ADMIN_TRACKERS_TO_WI8.02" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\05_timeline"; dest="WA_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW\WA0_00_COMMAND_MAP"; prefix="WA0.00.030"; rule="TIMELINE_TO_WA0.00" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\10_overviews"; dest="WE_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN\WE4_00_CHAIN_ANALYSIS"; prefix="WE4.00.010"; rule="OVERVIEWS_TO_WE4.00" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\20_strategy\10_ada_title_ii"; dest="WG_GROUNDS_ADA\WG6_00_ADA_STRATEGY"; prefix="WG6.00.010"; rule="ADA_STRATEGY_TO_WG6.00" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\20_strategy\20_jurisdiction_service_tr_4_1_b"; dest="WB_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW\WB1_00_LAW_RESEARCH"; prefix="WB1.00.010"; rule="SERVICE_LAW_TO_WB1.00" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\20_strategy\30_void_vs_voidable_tr_60b"; dest="WB_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW\WB1_00_LAW_RESEARCH"; prefix="WB1.00.020"; rule="VOID_LAW_TO_WB1.00" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\30_drafts-templates\10_motions"; dest="WC_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS\WC2_00_DRAFT_MOTIONS"; prefix="WC2.00.010"; rule="MOTION_DRAFTS_TO_WC2.00" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\30_drafts-templates\20_declarations_affidavits"; dest="WF_FACTS_DECLARATIONS\WF5_01_DRAFT_DECLARATIONS"; prefix="WF5.01.010"; rule="DECL_DRAFTS_TO_WF5.01" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\30_drafts-templates\50_proposed_orders"; dest="WC_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS\WC2_01_PROPOSED_ORDERS"; prefix="WC2.01.010"; rule="ORDERS_DRAFTS_TO_WC2.01" },
>   @{ src="00_admin\40_action_center"; dest="WA_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW\WA0_01_HEARING_PLANNING"; prefix="WA0.01.010"; rule="ACTION_CENTER_TO_WA0.01" },
> 
>   @{ src="10_filings"; dest="__INTAKE_FILINGS"; prefix="WZ9.00.050"; rule="FILINGS_INTAKE_TO_WZ" }, # staged; we’ll promote selectively
>   @{ src="20_evidence_vault"; dest="WH_HARD_EVIDENCE\WH7_00_RAW_INTAKE"; prefix="WH7.00.010"; rule="EVIDENCE_VAULT_TO_WH7.00" },
>   @{ src="30_court_record\10_docket"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_00_DOCKET_RECORD"; prefix="WI8.00.001"; rule="DOCKET_TO_WI8.00" },
> 
>   @{ src="personal_narrative\01_Public_Narrative"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_01_PUBLIC_ADVOCACY"; prefix="WI8.01.010"; rule="PUBLIC_NARR_TO_WI8.01" },
>   @{ src="personal_narrative\02_Exposure_and_Harm"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_02_DAMAGES_AND_SETTLEMENT"; prefix="WI8.02.050"; rule="HARM_TO_WI8.02" },
>   @{ src="personal_narrative\03_Internal_Analysis"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_99_INTERNAL_ONLY"; prefix="WI8.99.010"; rule="INTERNAL_ANALYSIS_TO_WI8.99" },
>   @{ src="personal_narrative\04_Donations_and_Support"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_01_PUBLIC_ADVOCACY"; prefix="WI8.01.050"; rule="DONATIONS_TO_WI8.01" },
>   @{ src="personal_narrative\05_Timeline"; dest="WA_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW\WA0_00_COMMAND_MAP"; prefix="WA0.00.060"; rule="NARR_TIMELINE_TO_WA0.00" },
> 
>   @{ src="tools"; dest="..\99_ARCHIVE\tools_legacy"; prefix="ARCH.010"; rule="TOOLS_TO_ARCHIVE" }
> )
> 
> # ---- Migration runner
> foreach ($m in $map) {
>   $srcRoot = Join-Path $legacyPath $m.src
> 
>   if (-not (Test-Path $srcRoot)) { continue }
> 
>   # Special case: tools -> archive path already relative in map
>   if ($m.rule -eq "TOOLS_TO_ARCHIVE") {
>     $dstBase = Join-Path $caseRoot "99_ARCHIVE\tools_legacy"
>   }
>   elseif ($m.dest -eq "__INTAKE_FILINGS") {
>     $dstBase = Join-Path $warRoot "WZ_PROMOTION_PIPELINE\WZ9.00.050_FILINGS_INTAKE"
>     Ensure-Dir $dstBase
>   }
>   else {
>     $dstBase = Join-Path $warRoot $m.dest
>     Ensure-Dir $dstBase
>   }
> 
>   Get-ChildItem -LiteralPath $srcRoot -Recurse -File | ForEach-Object {
>     $rel = $_.FullName.Substring($srcRoot.Length).TrimStart('\','/')
>     $destDir = Join-Path $dstBase (Split-Path $rel -Parent)
> 
>     $oldName = $_.Name
>     $newName = "{0}__{1}" -f $m.prefix, $oldName
>     $destPath = Join-Path $destDir $newName
> 
>     CopyOrMove $_.FullName $destPath $m.rule
>   }
> }
> 
> Write-Host "DONE. Migration complete. Log: $logPath"
> Write-Host "Mode: $mode | Hashing: $hash"
> ```
> 
> ### What this script intentionally does NOT do (on purpose)
> - It does **not** guess which filings belong in Court Binder tabs.  
>   That’s a **promotion decision** you make with the checklist, because it’s strategic/legal.
> 
> Instead it stages filings under:
> `02_WAR_ROOM/WZ_PROMOTION_PIPELINE/WZ9.00.050_FILINGS_INTAKE/`
> 
> Then you promote clean items into:
> `01_COURT_BINDER/...`
> 
> That’s the correct control.
> 
> ---
> 
> # 4) COURT BINDER PROMOTION TARGETS (QUICK MAP)
> 
> When you start promoting from War Room:
> 
> - Motions PDFs → `C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS/...`
> - Service returns / summons → `D_DELIVERY_SERVICE/...`
> - Writ / enforcement chain docs → `E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN/...`
> - ADA notice/support → `G_GROUNDS_ADA/...`
> - Exhibits A–H final → `H_HARD_EXHIBITS/H7_01_EXHIBITS_A_G/...`
> - Full docket (if needed) → `I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE/I8_01_FULL_DOCKET/...` (usually Blue only)
> 
> ---
> 
> # 5) COLOR BINDER CONTROL (MATCHES YOUR SYSTEM)
> 
> - **White (Judge):** print only from `01_COURT_BINDER/.../09_EXPORTS/COURT_SET/`
> - **Blue (You):** print from `.../09_EXPORTS/PERSONAL_MASTER/`
> - **Brown (Opposition):** print from `.../09_EXPORTS/OPPOSITION_SET/`
> - **Red (Internal):** print from `.../09_EXPORTS/INTERNAL_RED_SET/` and/or War Room internal notes  
>   (But ideally: Red binder is *not printed* unless you must—keep digital.)
> 
> ---
>

> Tell me **one thing**:
> 
> **Do you want the migration to run in `COPY` mode (recommended) or `MOVE` mode?**
> 
> If you answer “COPY”, you can run the script immediately without fear, and we’ll start building the **promotion shortlist** for the hearing packet.

### User
> why doesnt the script create the log files, im tired, lol, copy mode is better ill just archive legacy for emergency

### Assistant
> You’re right to call that out. My earlier builder script created placeholders but **did not actually write the promotion checklist or templates content**, and the migration script **assumed** the log existed (it created the CSV header, but didn’t create a notes file). That’s friction you don’t need when you’re tired.
> 
> Below is the **fixed, single “DO IT ALL” PowerShell script** for **COPY mode** that:
> 
> - Builds **Court Binder + War Room + Archive + Templates**
> - Creates **MIGRATION_LOG.csv** (with header)
> - Creates **MIGRATION_NOTES.md**
> - Creates **PROMOTION_CHECKLIST.md**
> - Creates **all Obsidian templates with real content**
> - Runs **legacy migration in COPY mode**
> - Writes a row for every file copied (and optionally SHA256)
> 
> You run this once and you’re done.
> 
> ---
> 
> ## ONE SCRIPT: BUILD + LOGS + TEMPLATES + CHECKLIST + MIGRATE (COPY)
> 
> ```powershell
> # ==========================================
> # FCFCU_CASE - Build + Logs + Templates + Checklist + Legacy Migration (COPY)
> # ==========================================
> param(
>   [string]$legacyPath = ".\__legacy",
>   [string]$caseRoot   = ".\FCFCU_CASE",
>   [bool]$hash = $true
> )
> 
> # ---------- Helpers ----------
> function Ensure-Dir($p){ New-Item -ItemType Directory -Force -Path $p | Out-Null }
> function Ensure-File($p, $content){
>   Ensure-Dir (Split-Path $p -Parent)
>   Set-Content -Path $p -Value $content -Encoding UTF8
> }
> function Append-Content($p, $content){
>   Ensure-Dir (Split-Path $p -Parent)
>   Add-Content -Path $p -Value $content -Encoding UTF8
> }
> function NowIso(){ (Get-Date).ToString("yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss") }
> function Sha256($p){
>   if (-not $hash) { return "" }
>   try { return (Get-FileHash -Algorithm SHA256 -Path $p).Hash } catch { return "" }
> }
> 
> # ---------- Roots ----------
> $courtRoot = Join-Path $caseRoot "01_COURT_BINDER\FCFCU-49D03-2501-MF-002559"
> $warRoot   = Join-Path $caseRoot "02_WAR_ROOM"
> $archRoot  = Join-Path $caseRoot "99_ARCHIVE"
> $tplDir    = Join-Path $caseRoot "03_OBSIDIAN_TEMPLATES"
> 
> Ensure-Dir $caseRoot
> Ensure-Dir $courtRoot
> Ensure-Dir $warRoot
> Ensure-Dir $archRoot
> Ensure-Dir $tplDir
> 
> # ---------- Logs (CREATE THEM, ALWAYS) ----------
> $logCsv = Join-Path $caseRoot "MIGRATION_LOG.csv"
> $logMd  = Join-Path $caseRoot "MIGRATION_NOTES.md"
> 
> if (-not (Test-Path $logCsv)) {
>   Ensure-File $logCsv "timestamp,action,src,dst,old_name,new_name,sha256,rule"
> }
> if (-not (Test-Path $logMd)) {
>   Ensure-File $logMd @"
> # Migration Notes
> Created: $(NowIso)
> 
> Purpose:
> - Preserve __legacy as an immutable snapshot.
> - Copy items into the new FCFCU_CASE structure.
> - Apply prefix-only renames for ordered continuity without rewriting history.
> 
> Non-negotiables:
> - __legacy is not modified (COPY mode).
> - New name = PREFIX + '__' + OriginalName
> - Every file copied is logged in MIGRATION_LOG.csv (optional SHA256).
> 
> "@
> }
> 
> function LogRow($action,$src,$dst,$old,$new,$h,$rule){
>   $line = "{0},{1},""{2}"",""{3}"",""{4}"",""{5}"",{6},""{7}""" -f (NowIso),$action,$src,$dst,$old,$new,$h,$rule
>   Append-Content $logCsv $line
> }
> 
> function CopyWithLog($src,$dst,$rule){
>   Ensure-Dir (Split-Path $dst -Parent)
>   Copy-Item -LiteralPath $src -Destination $dst -Force
>   $old = Split-Path $src -Leaf
>   $new = Split-Path $dst -Leaf
>   $h = Sha256 $dst
>   LogRow "COPY" $src $dst $old $new $h $rule
> }
> 
> # ---------- Promotion Checklist (WRITE CONTENT NOW) ----------
> $promotionChecklist = Join-Path $caseRoot "PROMOTION_CHECKLIST.md"
> $promotionChecklistWar = Join-Path $warRoot "WZ_PROMOTION_PIPELINE\WZ9.00.010_PROMOTION_CHECKLIST.md"
> 
> $promotionText = @"
> # Promotion Checklist (War Room → Court Binder)
> Status: LOCKED PROCEDURE
> 
> ## Definitions
> - **War Room file:** starts with `W` (e.g., `WD3...`, `WH7...`)
> - **Court Binder file:** identical code WITHOUT `W` (e.g., `D3...`, `H7...`)
> - **Promotion:** copy finalized item into Court Binder and remove `W`.
> 
> ## Rule 0 — Safety (red/internal stays red)
> If it contains ANY of:
> - strategy speculation
> - media/PR planning
> - settlement posture not filed
> - personal narrative
> - mental health / private life details
> - accusations not supported by exhibits
> → it **stays War Room** (internal/red only).
> 
> ## Rule 1 — Court relevance
> To promote, it must answer one of:
> - What is the legal issue?
> - What relief am I requesting?
> - What admissible fact supports it?
> - What docket item proves it?
> 
> If it doesn’t serve a hearing purpose, it stays War Room.
> 
> ## Rule 2 — Evidence hygiene (PDFs/images/video stills)
> Before promoting:
> - correct code/section and correct date
> - legible at 100% zoom and when printed
> - no unrelated pages included
> - keep an unmarked original in War Room if you highlight/annotate
> 
> ## Rule 3 — Sleeve rule (physical)
> Sleeve:
> - Tab H exhibits ALWAYS
> - official returns/orders/writs (Tabs D/E) usually YES
> - anything you may hand up YES
> No sleeve:
> - your summaries, indexes, scripts (hole-punch)
> 
> ## Rule 4 — Header rule (promoted markdown)
> Top must include:
> - code (e.g., `D3.03.001`)
> - title
> - purpose (1 sentence)
> - “Use in court” (what you will say)
> 
> ## Rule 5 — Copy procedure (no renumbering)
> 1) COPY war file into correct Court Binder folder  
> 2) REMOVE leading `W` from filename only  
> 3) Do NOT change numbering  
> 4) Add it to the appropriate Export Master
> 
> ## Rule 6 — Logging
> Record in:
> - `02_WAR_ROOM/WZ_PROMOTION_PIPELINE/WZ9.00.003_PROMOTION_LOG.md`
> Include: date, from, to, reason.
> 
> ## Rule 7 — Print sets
> Only print from Export Masters:
> - White: Court Set
> - Blue: Personal Master
> - Brown: Opposition Set
> - Red: Internal Red Set
> "@
> 
> Ensure-File $promotionChecklist $promotionText
> Ensure-File $promotionChecklistWar $promotionText
> 
> # ---------- Obsidian templates (WRITE CONTENT NOW) ----------
> Ensure-File (Join-Path $tplDir "TEMPLATE_SECTION_COVER.md") @"
> ---
> type: section_cover
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: {{TAB}}
> print: true
> sleeve: false
> ---
> 
> # {{CODE}} — {{TAB}} (Section Cover)
> 
> **Purpose:**  
> - 
> 
> **What the court should understand from this tab:**  
> - 
> - 
> 
> **What I’m asking for (if applicable):**  
> - 
> "@
> 
> Ensure-File (Join-Path $tplDir "TEMPLATE_SECTION_INDEX.md") @"
> ---
> type: section_index
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: {{TAB}}
> print: true
> sleeve: false
> ---
> 
> # {{CODE}} — {{TAB}} (Index)
> 
> ## Contents (in order)
> 1. 
> 2. 
> 3. 
> 
> ## Use in court (script)
> - ""Your Honor, this tab shows…""
> - ""The key document is…""
> "@
> 
> Ensure-File (Join-Path $tplDir "TEMPLATE_COURT_DOC.md") @"
> ---
> type: court_doc
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: {{TAB}}
> print: true
> sleeve: {{SLEEVE}}
> ---
> 
> # {{CODE}} — {{TITLE}}
> 
> **Purpose (1 sentence):**  
> -
> 
> **Use in court (what I will say):**  
> -
> 
> **Key points:**
> - 
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Cross-references:**
> - Exhibits:
> - Docket items:
> "@
> 
> Ensure-File (Join-Path $tplDir "TEMPLATE_WAR_NOTE.md") @"
> ---
> type: war_note
> code: {{WCODE}}
> tab: {{WTAB}}
> print: false
> internal: true
> ---
> 
> # {{WCODE}} — {{TITLE}} (WAR ROOM)
> 
> **Working hypothesis / goal:**  
> -
> 
> **Evidence to validate:**  
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Risks / pushback:**  
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Promotion candidate?**
> - [ ] Yes
> - [ ] No
> If yes, target court slot: {{TARGET_CODE}}
> "@
> 
> Ensure-File (Join-Path $tplDir "TEMPLATE_EXHIBIT_LABEL.md") @"
> ---
> type: exhibit_label
> code: {{CODE}}
> tab: H_HARD_EXHIBITS
> print: true
> sleeve: true

> 
> # {{CODE}} — EXHIBIT {{LETTER}}: {{TITLE}}

> **Source:**

> **Handling:**
> - keep in sleeve
> - hand-up ready
> "@
> 
> Ensure-File (Join-Path $tplDir "TEMPLATE_HANDUP_PACKET_NOTE.md") @"
> ---
> type: handup_packet
> print: true
> sleeve: true
> ---
> 
> # HAND-UP PACKET — {{PACKET_NAME}}
> 
> **When to hand up:**  
> -
> 
> **Contains (exact):**
> - 
> - 
> - 
> 
> **Instructions:**
> - Provide only upon request or at the moment referenced.
> "@
> 
> # ---------- Minimal Court + War scaffold (tabs + key folders) ----------
> $courtTabs = @(
>  "A_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW","B_BASIS_ISSUE_AND_LAW","C_CLAIMS_AND_MOTIONS","D_DELIVERY_SERVICE",
>  "E_EFFECTS_PROCEDURAL_CHAIN","F_FACTS_DECLARATIONS","G_GROUNDS_ADA","H_HARD_EXHIBITS","I_INTERNAL_REFERENCE",

> Ensure-File (Join-Path $courtRoot "09_EXPORTS\INTERNAL_RED_SET\00_INTERNAL_RED_MASTER.md") ""

> 
>   @{ src="personal_narrative\01_Public_Narrative"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_01_PUBLIC_ADVOCACY"; prefix="WI8.01.010"; rule="PUBLIC_NARR_TO_WI8.01" },

>   @{ src="personal_narrative\04_Donations_and_Support"; dest="WI_INTERNAL_REFERENCE\WI8_01_PUBLIC_ADVOCACY"; prefix="WI8.01.050"; rule="DONATIONS_TO_WI8.01" },
>   @{ src="personal_narrative\05_Timeline"; dest="WA_ANCHOR_OVERVIEW\WA0_00_COMMAND_MAP"; prefix="WA0.00.060"; rule="NARR_TIMELINE_TO_WA0.00" },
> 
>   @{ src="tools"; dest="..\99_ARCHIVE\tools_legacy"; prefix="ARCH.010"; rule="TOOLS_TO_ARCHIVE" }

> foreach ($m in $map) {
>   $srcRoot = Join-Path $legacyPath $m.src
>   if (-not (Test-Path $srcRoot)) { continue }
> 
>   $dstBase =
>     if ($m.rule -eq "TOOLS_TO_ARCHIVE") { Join-Path $caseRoot "99_ARCHIVE\tools_legacy" }
>     else { Join-Path $warRoot $m.dest }

>
